\chapter{Data from Stack Overflow}

This appendix shows plots and tables regarding the fitting, residual-based correction and evaluation for the data from Stack Overflow. In this you will find sections for each time grouping (week or month), sub-sections for each language, which are divided into inner sections for each time slice (100\%, 90\%, 80\%, 70\% and 60\%).

\newpage


\section{Week}

\subsection{Assembly}

\subsubsection{Time slice 100\%}

\begin{center} 
\captionof{table}{Fit parameters, $R^2$ and p-value for the original model and corrections (language Assembly, grouped by week, 100\% of the dataset)} 
\label{my-label} 
\begin{tabular}{l|c|c|c|c|c|c} 
\hline
\multicolumn{1}{c|}{\multirow{2}{*}{Model}} & \multicolumn{4}{c|}{\begin{tabular}[c]{@{}c@{}}Fit Parameters\\ (original/correction)\end{tabular}} & \multicolumn{1}{c|}{\multirow{2}{*}{$R^2$}} & \multicolumn{1}{c}{\multirow{2}{*}{\begin{tabular}[c]{@{}c@{}}SE\\ p-value\end{tabular}}} \\ \cline{2-5} 
\multicolumn{1}{c|}{} & K/a & \multicolumn{1}{c|}{r/f} & \multicolumn{1}{c|}{$t_m$/q} & \multicolumn{1}{c|}{a/s} & \multicolumn{1}{c|}{} & \multicolumn{1}{c}{} \\ \hline 
Original & 29561.632021 & 0.004866 & -2396.936026 & $1.442054\times10^{-6}$ & 0.999757 & $\approx$ 1.0 \\
Correction 1 & 75.5346 & 0.004815 & 4.96211 & 91.5837 & 0.999849 & $\approx$ 1.0 \\ 
Correction 2 & 55.9015 & 0.019391 & 24.5318 & 234.455 & 0.999913 & $\approx$ 1.0 \\ 
Correction 3 & 46.8068 & 0.014996 & 2.56276 & 155.248 & 0.999919 & $\approx$ 1.0 \\ \hline 
\end{tabular} 
\end{center} 

\begin{center}
{\includegraphics[width=\textwidth]{figures/stackoverflow-week/assembly100_finalCorrectedGaussian.eps}}
\captionof{figure}{Result after thir iteration of residual-based correction, for language Assembly, grouped by week, time slice 100\%.}
\end{center}
